ay=ax;
}

}
}
}

}

--- Raw source ---
(V,W){
if((%IS_VAR(this)===null)||(this===(void 0)))throw MakeTypeError(15,"String.prototype.subString");
var K=((typeof(%IS_VAR(this))==='string')?this:$nonStringToString(this));
var ax=K.length;
var ay=(%_IsSmi(%IS_VAR(V))?V:%NumberToInteger(o(V)));
if(ay<0){
ay=0;
}else if(ay>ax){
ay=ax;
}
var az=ax;
if(!(W===(void 0))){
az=(%_IsSmi(%IS_VAR(W))?W:%NumberToInteger(o(W)));
if(az>ax){
az=ax;
}else{
if(az<0)az=0;
if(ay>az){
var aK=az;
az=ay;
ay=aK;
}
}
}
return %_SubString(K,ay,az);
}

--- Raw source ---
(V,W){
if((%IS_VAR(this)===null)||(this===(void 0)))throw MakeTypeError(15,"String.prototype.subString");
var K=((typeof(%IS_VAR(this))==='string')?this:$nonStringToString(this));
var ax=K.length;
var ay=(%_IsSmi(%IS_VAR(V))?V:%NumberToInteger(o(V)));
if(ay<0){
ay=0;
}else if(ay>ax){
ay=ax;
}
var az=ax;
if(!(W===(void 0))){
az=(%_IsSmi(%IS_VAR(W))?W:%NumberToInteger(o(W)));
if(az>ax){
az=ax;
}else{
if(az<0)az=0;
if(ay>az){
var aK=az;
az=ay;
ay=aK;
}
}
}
return %_SubString(K,ay,az);
}

--- Raw source ---
(K,x,D){
if((K===(void 0))){
K=',';
}else if(!(typeof(K)==='string')){
K=$nonStringToString(K);
}
var V=%_FastOneByteArrayJoin(x,K);
if(!(V===(void 0)))return V;
if(D===1){
var C=x[0];
if((typeof(C)==='string'))return C;
if((C==null))return'';
return $nonStringToString(C);
}
return Join(x,D,K,ConvertToString);
}
